debits  £104245.20 [POW-U] Total  credits  £100540.29 [PID-U] Closing  balance  £4932.88 [CB-U] Important 
information  about  compensation  arrangements  We  are  covered  by  the 
Financial  Services  Compensation  Scheme  (FSCS).
The  FSCS  can  pay  compensation  to  depositors  if  a  bank  is  unable  to  meet  its  financial  obligations.
Your  deposit  is  covered  by  the  scheme.
Details  on  the  protection  of  eligible  deposits  can  be 
found  in  the  information  sheet  and  deposits  excluded  from 
the  scheme  can  be  found  in  the  exclusion  list 
which  can  be  obtained  from  your  local  branch.
For  further  information  about  the  compensation  provided  by  the  FSCS,  refer  to  the  FSCS  website  at  www.FSCS.org.uk.
Interest  rate  information  Arranged  Overdraft  interest  rates  apply  to 
the  amount  of  any  borrowing,  up  to  your  Arranged 
Overdraft  limit.
Unarranged  Overdraft  interest  rates  apply  to  any  borrowing  which 
is  the  result  of  our  agreeing  to  a  request 
from  you  for  a  temporary  Unarranged  Overdraft  or  temporary 
increase  to  an  existing  Arranged  Overdraft  to  cover  a 
payment  despite  lack  of  funds.
Interest  rates  applicable  during  the  statement  period  are  available 
on  request,  please  call  the  team  at  Yorkshire  Bank 
on  <  strong>0800  456  1247<  /strong>  or  <  strong>+44 
141  951  7315<  /strong>.
Dispute  resolution  If  you  have  a  complaint,  please  talk 
to  us  first  so  that  we  can  try  to 
resolve  it.
If  you  are  not  happy  with  the  way  we 
handled  your  complaint  or  the  result,  you  can  then 
refer  the  matter  to  the  Financial  Ombudsman  Service.
The  Financial  Ombudsman  Service  is  an  independent  organisation  that 
helps  resolve  complaints  that  customers  and  financial  institutions  haven't 
been  able  to  solve  themselves.

£89653.01 [PID-U] Closing  balance  £1841.35 [CB-U] Important  information  about  compensation  arrangements 
We  are  covered  by  the  Financial  Services  Compensation  Scheme 
(FSCS).
The  FSCS  can  pay  compensation  to  depositors  if  a  bank  is  unable  to  meet  its  financial  obligations.
Your  deposit  is  covered  by  the  scheme.
Details  on  the  protection  of  eligible  deposits  can  be 
found  in  the  information  sheet  and  deposits  excluded  from 
the  scheme  can  be  found  in  the  exclusion  list 
which  can  be  obtained  from  your  local  branch.
For  further  information  about  the  compensation  provided  by  the  FSCS,  refer  to  the  FSCS  website  at  www.FSCS.org.uk.
Interest  rate  information  Arranged  Overdraft  interest  rates  apply  to 
the  amount  of  any  borrowing,  up  to  your  Arranged 
Overdraft  limit.
Unarranged  Overdraft  interest  rates  apply  to  any  borrowing  which 
is  the  result  of  our  agreeing  to  a  request 
from  you  for  a  temporary  Unarranged  Overdraft  or  temporary 
increase  to  an  existing  Arranged  Overdraft  to  cover  a 
payment  despite  lack  of  funds.
Interest  rates  applicable  during  the  statement  period  are  available 
on  request,  please  call  the  team  at  Yorkshire  Bank 
on  <  strong>0800  456  1247<  /strong>  or  <  strong>+44 
141  951  7315<  /strong>.
Dispute  resolution  If  you  have  a  complaint,  please  talk 
to  us  first  so  that  we  can  try  to 
resolve  it.
If  you  are  not  happy  with  the  way  we 
handled  your  complaint  or  the  result,  you  can  then 
refer  the  matter  to  the  Financial  Ombudsman  Service.
The  Financial  Ombudsman  Service  is  an  independent  organisation  that 
helps  resolve  complaints  that  customers  and  financial  institutions  haven't 
been  able  to  solve  themselves.

credits  £157370.10 [PID-U] Closing  balance  £3940.20 [CB-U] Important  information  about  compensation 
arrangements  We  are  covered  by  the  Financial  Services  Compensation 
Scheme  (FSCS).
The  FSCS  can  pay  compensation  to  depositors  if  a  bank  is  unable  to  meet  its  financial  obligations.
Your  deposit  is  covered  by  the  scheme.
Details  on  the  protection  of  eligible  deposits  can  be 
found  in  the  information  sheet  and  deposits  excluded  from 
the  scheme  can  be  found  in  the  exclusion  list 
which  can  be  obtained  from  your  local  branch.
For  further  information  about  the  compensation  provided  by  the  FSCS,  refer  to  the  FSCS  website  at  www.FSCS.org.uk.
Interest  rate  information  Arranged  Overdraft  interest  rates  apply  to 
the  amount  of  any  borrowing,  up  to  your  Arranged 
Overdraft  limit.
Unarranged  Overdraft  interest  rates  apply  to  any  borrowing  which 
is  the  result  of  our  agreeing  to  a  request 
from  you  for  a  temporary  Unarranged  Overdraft  or  temporary 
increase  to  an  existing  Arranged  Overdraft  to  cover  a 
payment  despite  lack  of  funds.
Interest  rates  applicable  during  the  statement  period  are  available 
on  request,  please  call  the  team  at  Yorkshire  Bank 
on  <  strong>0800  456  1247<  /strong>  or  <  strong>+44 
141  951  7315<  /strong>.
Dispute  resolution  If  you  have  a  complaint,  please  talk 
to  us  first  so  that  we  can  try  to 
resolve  it.
If  you  are  not  happy  with  the  way  we 
handled  your  complaint  or  the  result,  you  can  then 
refer  the  matter  to  the  Financial  Ombudsman  Service.
The  Financial  Ombudsman  Service  is  an  independent  organisation  that 
helps  resolve  complaints  that  customers  and  financial  institutions  haven't 
been  able  to  solve  themselves.

arrangements  We  are  covered  by  the  Financial  Services  Compensation 
Scheme  (FSCS).
The  FSCS  can  pay  compensation  to  depositors  if  a  bank  is  unable  to  meet  its  financial  obligations.
Your  deposit  is  covered  by  the  scheme.
Details  on  the  protection  of  eligible  deposits  can  be 
found  in  the  information  sheet  and  deposits  excluded  from 
the  scheme  can  be  found  in  the  exclusion  list 
which  can  be  obtained  from  your  local  branch.
For  further  information  about  the  compensation  provided  by  the  FSCS,  refer  to  the  FSCS  website  at  www.FSCS.org.uk.
Interest  rate  information  Arranged  Overdraft  interest  rates  apply  to 
the  amount  of  any  borrowing,  up  to  your  Arranged 
Overdraft  limit.
Unarranged  Overdraft  interest  rates  apply  to  any  borrowing  which 
is  the  result  of  our  agreeing  to  a  request 
from  you  for  a  temporary  Unarranged  Overdraft  or  temporary 
increase  to  an  existing  Arranged  Overdraft  to  cover  a 
payment  despite  lack  of  funds.
Interest  rates  applicable  during  the  statement  period  are  available 
on  request,  please  call  the  team  at  Yorkshire  Bank 
on  <  strong>0800  456  1247<  /strong>  or  <  strong>+44 
141  951  7315<  /strong>.

to  us  first  so  that  we  can  try  to 
resolve  it.
If  you  are  not  happy  with  the  way  we 
handled  your  complaint  or  the  result,  you  can  then 
refer  the  matter  to  the  Financial  Ombudsman  Service.
The  Financial  Ombudsman  Service  is  an  independent  organisation  that 
helps  resolve  complaints  that  customers  and  financial  institutions  haven't 
been  able  to  solve  themselves.

£50135.62 [PID-U] Closing  balance  £2162.70 [B-U] Important  information  about  compensation  arrangements 
We  are  covered  by  the  Financial  Services  Compensation  Scheme 
(FSCS).
The  FSCS  can  pay  compensation  to  depositors  if  a  bank  is  unable  to  meet  its  financial  obligations.
Your  deposit  is  covered  by  the  scheme.
Details  on  the  protection  of  eligible  deposits  can  be 
found  in  the  information  sheet  and  deposits  excluded  from 
the  scheme  can  be  found  in  the  exclusion  list 
which  can  be  obtained  from  your  local  branch.
For  further  information  about  the  compensation  provided  by  the  FSCS,  refer  to  the  FSCS  website  at  www.FSCS.org.uk.
Interest  rate  information  Arranged  Overdraft  interest  rates  apply  to 
the  amount  of  any  borrowing,  up  to  your  Arranged 
Overdraft  limit.
Unarranged  Overdraft  interest  rates  apply  to  any  borrowing  which 
is  the  result  of  our  agreeing  to  a  request 
from  you  for  a  temporary  Unarranged  Overdraft  or  temporary 
increase  to  an  existing  Arranged  Overdraft  to  cover  a 
payment  despite  lack  of  funds.
Interest  rates  applicable  during  the  statement  period  are  available 
on  request,  please  call  the  team  at  Yorkshire  Bank 
on  <  strong>0800  456  1247<  /strong>  or  <  strong>+44 
141  951  7315<  /strong>.
Dispute  resolution  If  you  have  a  complaint,  please  talk 
to  us  first  so  that  we  can  try  to 
resolve  it.
If  you  are  not  happy  with  the  way  we 
handled  your  complaint  or  the  result,  you  can  then 
refer  the  matter  to  the  Financial  Ombudsman  Service.
The  Financial  Ombudsman  Service  is  an  independent  organisation  that 
helps  resolve  complaints  that  customers  and  financial  institutions  haven't 
been  able  to  solve  themselves.
